    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><span style="white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</span></p></td>
    <td style="padding-top:0.01in;vertical-align:top;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:4.3pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4.3pt;text-align:left;"><span style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth Finance Corp.</span></p></td>

 <body style="margin: auto!important;padding: 8px;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;min-height:0.5in;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><img src="img251088904_0.jpg" alt="img251088904_0.jpg" style="width:187px;height:38px;">&#160;</p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:14pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth Finance Corp. Reports Fourth Quarter and Fiscal Year Ended 2023 Financial Results</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Delivered Total and Net Investment Income of $39.2 million and $18.3 million, Respectively</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Investment Portfolio of $1.0 billion</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call Today, Thursday, March 7, 2024 at 5:00 p.m. ET</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">MENLO PARK, Calif., March 7, 2024&#x2014;Runway Growth Finance Corp. (Nasdaq: RWAY) </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">(&#x201c;Runway Growth&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;),</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> a leading provider of flexible capital solutions to late- and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity, today announced its financial results for the fourth quarter and fiscal year ended December 31, 2023.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Fourth Quarter 2023 Highlights</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment income of $39.2 million </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net investment income of $18.3 million, or $0.45 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net asset value of $13.50 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Dollar-weighted annualized yield on debt investments of 16.9% for the quarter</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Eight investments completed in new and existing portfolio companies, representing $154.6 million in funded loans and other investments</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:0;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Aggregate proceeds of $63.4 million received from principal prepayments </font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">2023 Fiscal Year Highlights</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment portfolio at year-end 2023 of $1.0 billion at fair value, excluding US Treasury Bills</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net investment income of $78.3 million, or $1.93 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net asset value (&#x201c;NAV&#x201d;) at 12/31/2023 of $547.1 million, or $13.50 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment fundings of $259.2 million: $83.5 million in four new portfolio companies and $175.7 million in </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">14</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> existing portfolio companies</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Low credit loss ratio of an average 14 basis points per year on a gross basis and an average 11 basis points per year on a net (debt and equity) basis, based on cumulative commitments since inception</font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">First Quarter 2024 Distributions</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Declared first quarter 2024 regular dividend of $0.40 per share</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:6pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:6pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Declared first quarter 2024 supplemental dividend of $0.07 per share </font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="flex-direction:column;display:flex;min-height:0.5in;justify-content:flex-end;"></div>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;min-height:0.5in;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><img src="img251088904_0.jpg" alt="img251088904_0.jpg" style="width:187px;height:38px;">&#160;</p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;In 2023, Runway Growth drove shareholder return while taking a measured approach to portfolio management as we preserved industry-leading credit quality,&#x201d; said Greg Greifeld,</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Acting Chief Executive Officer of Runway Growth, and Deputy Chief Investment Officer and Head of Credit of Runway Growth Capital. &#x201c;Over the course of the year, Runway Growth expanded its return on equity by 33 basis points and ended the fourth quarter with eight investments in new and existing portfolio companies.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Greifeld continued, &#x201c;We are proud of our team&#x2019;s thoughtful due diligence, consistent partnership with borrowers, and the momentum we delivered to end the year. We have applied a critical lens to evaluating our pipeline of opportunities, and are in a position to originate attractive investments that meet our high credit bar in the year ahead. Runway Growth is committed to generating shareholder value, which is reinforced by our strong and consistent base dividend and ongoing supplemental distributions.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Fourth Quarter 2023 Operating Results</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total investment income for the quarter ended </font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">December 31, 2023</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> was $39.2 million, compared to $36.5 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2022.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net investment income for the quarter ended December 31, 2023 was $18.3 million, or $0.45 per share, compared to $18.4 million, or $0.45 per share, for the quarter ended December 21, 2022.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company's dollar-weighted annualized yield on average debt investments for the quarter ended </font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> December 31, 2023,</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> was 16.9%</font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">. </font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company calculates the yield on dollar-weighted debt investments for any period measured as (1) total investment-related income during the period divided by (2) the daily average of the fair value of debt investments outstanding during the period.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Total operating expenses for the quarter ended </font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">December 31, 2023</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> were $20.9 million, compared to $18.1 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2022. The increase was driven by higher interest rates and increased financing expenses on borrowings.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net realized loss on investments was $17.2 million for the quarter ended </font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">December 31, 2023</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">, compared to a net realized loss of $2.0 million for the quarter ended December 31, 2022.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">For the quarter ended December 31, 2023, net change in unrealized loss on investments was $5.9 million, compared to a net change in unrealized gain of $2.1 million for the comparable prior year period.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Portfolio and Investment Activity</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">As of </font><font style="color:#231f20;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">December 31, 2023</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">, Runway Growth&#x2019;s investment portfolio had an aggregate fair value of approximately $1.0 billion and was comprised of approximately $978.5 million in term loans, 98.5% of which are senior secured loans and $46.5 million in warrants and other equity-related investments in 52 portfolio companies.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">During the fourth quarter of 2023, Runway Growth completed eight investments in new and existing portfolio companies, representing $154.6 million in funded loans.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">As of December 31, 2023, net asset value (&#x201c;NAV&#x2019;&#x201d;) per share was $13.50, compared to $14.22 as of December 31, 2022. Total net assets at the end of the quarter of 2023 was $547.1 million, down 5.0% from $576.1 million in the prior year period.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">For the quarter ended December 31, 2023, net decrease in net assets resulting from operations was $4.8 million, or $0.12 per share, compared to a net increase in net assets of $18.5 million, or $0.46 per share, for the quarter ended December 31, 2022.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Liquidity and Capital Resources</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">As of December 31, 2023, the Company had approximately $281.0 million in available liquidity, including unrestricted cash and cash equivalents of $3.0 million and $278.0 million in available borrowing capacity under the Company&#x2019;s credit facility, subject to existing terms, advance rates and regulatory and covenant requirements.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company ended the quarter with a core leverage ratio of approximately 95%, compared to 79% for the quarter ended September 30, 2023.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Distributions</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On February 1, 2024, the Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared a regular quarterly distribution of $0.40 per share for the first quarter of 2024, payable on February 28, 2024, to stockholders of record as of February 12, 2024. In addition, the Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared a supplemental dividend of $0.07 per share for the first quarter of 2024 that is also payable on February 28, 2024, to stockholders of record as of February 12, 2024.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Share Repurchase Program</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On November 2, 2023, the Company&#x2019;s board of directors approved a share repurchase program (the &#x201c;Share Repurchase Program&#x201d;) under which the Company may repurchase up to $25.0 million of its outstanding common stock. Under the Share Repurchase Program, purchases may be made at management&#x2019;s discretion from time to time in open-market transactions, in accordance with applicable securities laws and regulations.</font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="flex-direction:column;display:flex;min-height:0.5in;justify-content:flex-end;"></div>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <div style="padding-top:0.5in;min-height:0.5in;box-sizing:border-box;"><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><img src="img251088904_0.jpg" alt="img251088904_0.jpg" style="width:187px;height:38px;">&#160;</p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Recent Developments</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Company evaluated events subsequent to December 31, 2023 through March 7, 2024, the date the consolidated financial statements were issued.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Effective January 1, 2024, the Company placed one loan to Mingle Healthcare Solutions, Inc. on non-accrual status, representing an outstanding principal of $4.3 million at a fair market value of $3.8 million as of December 31, 2023. The loan comprised 0.37% of the total fair value of the Company's investment portfolio, excluding U.S. Treasury Bills, as of December 31, 2023.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On February 14, 2024, the Company received a partial prepayment of $7.1 million from MarleySpoon SE on its senior secured loan.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">On March 7, 2024, the Company and Cadma Capital Partners LLC entered into a Limited Liability Company Agreement to co-manage Runway-Cadma I LLC (the &#34;Joint Venture&#34;). The Joint Venture is expected to invest in various types of investments, including, but not limited to, first and second lien senior secured term loans, including delayed draw and multi-tranche loans, and secured revolving credit facilities.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">  </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth will hold a conference call to discuss its fourth quarter and fiscal year ended December 31, 2023, financial results at 2:00 p.m. PT (5:00 p.m. ET) on Thursday, March 7, 2024. To participate in the conference call or webcast, participants should register online at the </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Investor Relations website</font></font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">. The earnings call can also be accessed through the following links:</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:8pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:8pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Conference Call</font></font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;display:flex;margin-top:8pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:8pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10pt;font-family:Times New Roman;min-width:3.447919145106397%;display:inline-flex;justify-content:flex-start;">&#x2022;</font><div style="width:100%;display:inline;"><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Webcast</font></font></div></div>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">A live webcast will be available in the investor section of the </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Company&#x2019;s website</font></font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">, and will be archived for 90 days following the call.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:4pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About Runway Growth Finance Corp.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:8pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:8pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Runway Growth is a growing specialty finance company focused on providing flexible capital solutions to late- and growth-stage companies seeking an alternative to raising equity. Runway Growth is a closed-end investment fund that has elected to be regulated as a business development company under the Investment Company Act of 1940. Runway Growth is externally managed by Runway Growth Capital LLC, an established registered investment advisor that was formed in 2015 and led by industry veteran David Spreng. For more information, please visit </font><font><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">www.runwaygrowth.com</font></font><font style="color:#222222;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:'Calibri',sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></p>
